üìéFacilities:

The hotel still needs to strengthen management.
2 I walked around in southern Fujian. Compared with hotels of the same grade and price, I feel that there should be automatic curtains or automatic toilets here. Or midnight snack~
3 The hotel is on the flight path. You can occasionally hear airplane noises at night (the hotel has clearly informed you of this before). The latest is about 12:30, but the noise is not too loud and does not affect your rest
4 The pool is obviously large but the faucet head is very short (as shown in the picture). When washing hands and things, I always rub against the edge of the pool üò≠ a bit unscientific
The overall experience is good and I will recommend it to friends
